remove_multi_party_government_reforms = {

		remove_faction = conservative_party
		remove_faction = communist_party
		remove_faction = liberal_party
		remove_faction = social_democratic_party
		remove_faction = nationalist_party
		remove_faction = national_socialist_party	

}

check_southernsea_occupy = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = flg_southernsea_a_occupy
			}		
				clr_country_flag = flg_southernsea_a_occupy
				clr_country_flag = defense_war_southern_a
				clr_country_flag = flg_southernsea_a_100_done	
				set_variable = { which = pop_southernsea_a value = 0 }
				clear_global_event_target = tag_southernsea_a_opp
				clear_global_event_target = tag_southernsea_a_occupy
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = flg_southernsea_b_occupy
			}		
				clr_country_flag = flg_southernsea_b_occupy
				clr_country_flag = defense_war_southern_b
				clr_country_flag = flg_southernsea_b_100_done	
				set_variable = { which = pop_southernsea_b value = 0 }
				clear_global_event_target = tag_southernsea_b_opp
				clear_global_event_target = tag_southernsea_b_occupy
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = flg_southernsea_c_occupy
			}		
				clr_country_flag = flg_southernsea_c_occupy
				clr_country_flag = defense_war_southern_c
				clr_country_flag = flg_southernsea_c_100_done	
				set_variable = { which = pop_southernsea_c value = 0 }
				clear_global_event_target = tag_southernsea_c_opp
				clear_global_event_target = tag_southernsea_c_occupy
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = flg_southernsea_d_occupy
			}		
				clr_country_flag = flg_southernsea_d_occupy
				clr_country_flag = defense_war_southern_d
				clr_country_flag = flg_southernsea_d_100_done	
				set_variable = { which = pop_southernsea_d value = 0 }
				clear_global_event_target = tag_southernsea_d_opp
				clear_global_event_target = tag_southernsea_d_occupy
		}
}

			limit = {
				NOT = { industrialization = 90 }
			}
			set_variable = {

				value = 20
			}

				value = 20
			}

				value = 45
			}

			clr_province_flag = flg_industry_low
			set_province_flag = flg_industry_high
		}
	}

#province scope 	
building_adjust_pov_limit = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_province_flag = flg_add_road
		}
		clr_province_flag = flg_add_road			
		change_variable = {
			which = var_adm_limit
			value = 1
		}
		change_variable = {
			which = var_dip_limit
			value = 1
		}	
		change_variable = {
			which = var_mil_limit
			value = 1
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_province_flag = flg_add_highway
		}
		clr_province_flag = flg_add_highway			
		change_variable = {
			which = var_adm_limit
			value = 2
		}
		change_variable = {
			which = var_dip_limit
			value = 2
		}	
		change_variable = {
			which = var_mil_limit

		}
		
	}

		limit = {
			has_province_flag = flg_add_railroad
		}
		clr_province_flag = flg_add_railroad

			which = var_adm_limit

		change_variable = {
			which = var_dip_limit

			value = 5
		}
	}		
####################################################
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_province_flag = flg_clr_road
		}
		clr_province_flag = flg_clr_road			
		subtract_variable = {
			which = var_adm_limit
			value = 1
		}
		subtract_variable = {
			which = var_dip_limit
			value = 1
		}

			which = var_mil_limit
			value = 1
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_province_flag = flg_clr_highway
		}
		clr_province_flag = flg_clr_highway			
		subtract_variable = {
			which = var_adm_limit
			value = 2
		}
		subtract_variable = {
			which = var_dip_limit
			value = 2

reload_pov_limit = {
	export_to_variable = {
		which = var_pov_adm
		value = base_tax
	}
	export_to_variable = {
		which = var_pov_dip
		value = base_production
	}
	export_to_variable = {
		which = var_pov_mil
		value = base_manpower
	}					
}

remove_all_building = {
	if = {
		limit = { has_building = anti_nuclear } 
		remove_building = anti_nuclear 
	}		
	if = {
		limit = { has_building = special_mil_research }

pov_update_anti_nuclear_modifier = {
	hidden_effect = {
		owner = {
			remove_country_modifier = keep_1_anti_nuclear_building
			remove_country_modifier = keep_2_anti_nuclear_building
			remove_country_modifier = keep_3_anti_nuclear_building
			remove_country_modifier = keep_4_anti_nuclear_building
			remove_country_modifier = keep_5_anti_nuclear_building
			remove_country_modifier = keep_6_anti_nuclear_building
			remove_country_modifier = keep_7_anti_nuclear_building
			remove_country_modifier = keep_8_anti_nuclear_building
			remove_country_modifier = keep_9_anti_nuclear_building
			remove_country_modifier = keep_10_anti_nuclear_building
		}	
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					NOT = {
						calc_true_if = {
							all_owned_province = {
								has_building = anti_nuclear
							}
							amount = 1
						}
					}
				}
			}
			owner = {
				set_variable = {
					which = num_of_anti_nuclear
					value = 0
				}	
			}	
		}

			limit = {

jap_wii_termless_surrender_effect = {
	
	remove_government_reform = fascist_dictatorship
	change_religion = liberalism
	add_government_reform = english_monarchy
	
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_modifier = md_three_months
		}			
		remove_country_modifier = md_three_months
	}	
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_modifier = md_fanaticism_war
		}			
		remove_country_modifier = md_fanaticism_war
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = { has_global_flag = JA1_wii_fail }
		}		
		set_global_flag = JA1_wii_fail
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			exists = USA
		}		
		USA = {
			set_country_flag = win_wii_with_JA1
		}
	}	
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = flg_pearl_harbeor_success
		}		
		clr_country_flag = flg_pearl_harbeor_success
	}	
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = flg_need_more_source
		}		
		clr_country_flag = flg_need_more_source
	}		
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = flg_army_supported_occur
		}		
		clr_country_flag = flg_army_supported_occur
	}			

	every_owned_province = {
		limit = { 
			NOT = { region = japan_region }
		}
			remove_core = ROOT
			cede_province = ZZ3
	}
	every_province = {
		limit = { 
			region = japan_region
			owner = {
				NOT = {
					tag = ROOT	
				}	
			}
		}
		cede_province = ROOT
	}		
	ZZ3 = {
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = "md_no_occupy_tag"
			duration = -1
		}
		define_ruler = {
			name = "--------"
			adm = -1
			dip = -1
			mil = -1
			fixed = yes
    	}
		remove_ruler_all_personality = yes		
		add_ruler_personality = immortal_personality
	}	
	if = { 
		limit = {
			MCK = { num_of_cities = 1 }
			MCK = { ai = yes }
		}	
			CW1 = { inherit = MCK }
	}	
	#---- feedback taiwan -----
	if = { 
		limit = {
			exists = CHN
			NOT = { exists = ROC }
		}			
		every_province = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					area = taiwan_north_area
					area = taiwan_south_area
				}	
			}
				cede_province = CHN
		}	
	}
	if = { 
		limit = {
			OR = {
				exists = ROC
				AND = {
					NOT = { exists = ROC }
					NOT = { exists = CHN }
				}						
			}	
		}
		every_province = {
			limit = { 
				OR = {
					area = taiwan_north_area
					area = taiwan_south_area
				}
			}
				cede_province = ROC
		}	
	}	
			
	#####################################	
	if = { 
		limit = {
			any_owned_province = {
				has_province_modifier = army_supported_province
			}
		}
		clear_global_event_target = jap_support_province 
		every_owned_province = {
			limit = {
				has_province_modifier = army_supported_province
			}
				remove_province_modifier = army_supported_province
		}
	}
	#---- let korea individual
	# SOUTH_KOREA = 2512 734	3307	735	3308 1013	2511	736	3310	3311	3309	737
	# NORTH_KOREA = 3312 3313	3314 3315	3316 733	732	2513	2514	2515	1845
	every_province = { 
		limit = {
			OR = {
				province_id = 	2512
				province_id = 	734
				province_id = 	3307
				province_id = 	735
				province_id = 	3308
				province_id = 	1013
				province_id = 	2511
				province_id = 	736
				province_id = 	3310
				province_id = 	3311
				province_id = 	3309
				province_id = 	737		
			}	
		}
				cede_province = SKO
				add_core = SKO
	}
	every_province = { 
		limit = {
			OR = {
				province_id = 3312
				province_id = 3313
				province_id = 3314
				province_id = 3315
				province_id = 3316
				province_id = 733
				province_id = 732
				province_id = 2513
				province_id = 2514
				province_id = 2515
				province_id = 1845
	
			}	
		}
			cede_province = NOK
			add_core = NOK
	
	}
	#ROC CW1 對ZZ3 war
	if = {
		limit = {
			exists = ROC 
		}	
		ROC = {
			declare_war = ZZ3
		}
	}	
	if = {
		limit = {
			exists = CW1 
		}	
		CW1 = {
			declare_war = ZZ3
		}
	}
	######################################
	# connect to xy events / decisions
	######################################
	set_global_flag = flg_jap_wii_termless_surrender
}

#珍珠港事件之后的东西关系国家变化
wii_alliance_east_effect = {

	if = {
		limit = { 
			exists = ROC
		}
		GBR = {
			add_opinion = { 
				who = ROC
				modifier = op_same_enemy_atwar 
			}
			create_alliance = ROC
		}
		USA = {
			add_opinion = { 
				who = ROC
				modifier = op_same_enemy_atwar 
			}
			create_alliance = ROC
		}
		FR2 = {
			add_opinion = { 
				who = ROC
				modifier = op_same_enemy_atwar 
			}
			create_alliance = ROC
		}		
	}	
	if = {
		limit = { 
			exists = JX1
		}
		GBR = {
			add_opinion = { 
				who = JX1
				modifier = op_same_enemy_atwar 
			}
		}
		USA = {
			add_opinion = { 
				who = JX1
				modifier = op_same_enemy_atwar 
			}
		}		
	}
	if = {
		limit = { 
			exists = GX1
		}
		GBR = {
			add_opinion = { 
				who = GX1
				modifier = op_same_enemy_atwar 
			}
		}
		USA = {
			add_opinion = { 
				who = GX1
				modifier = op_same_enemy_atwar 
			}
		}		
	}
	if = {
		limit = { 
			exists = CW1
		}
		SOV = {
			add_opinion = { 
				who = CW1
				modifier = op_same_enemy_atwar 
			}
			create_alliance = CW1
		}			
	}
	if = {
		limit = { 
			exists = DX2
		}
		GBR = {
			add_opinion = { 
				who = DX2
				modifier = op_same_enemy_atwar 
			}
		}	
		USA = {
			add_opinion = { 
				who = DX2
				modifier = op_same_enemy_atwar 
			}
		}		
	}
}

ger_wii_termless_surrender_effect = {
		#xy new religion
		change_religion = liberalism
		every_province = {
			limit = { 
				has_province_flag = flg_nz1_start_provinces
				owner = { NOT = { tag = NZ1 } }
			}
				cede_province = NZ1
				add_core = NZ1
		}	
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_global_flag = NZ1_wii_fail }
			}		
			set_global_flag = NZ1_wii_fail
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				exists = USA
			}		
			USA = {
				set_country_flag = win_wii_with_NZ1
			}
		}		
	#clear the GER_md_fanaticism_war
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_modifier = md_fanaticism_war_GER
			}
				remove_country_modifier = md_fanaticism_war_GER
		}
	#clear clr_country_flag = flg_Hindenburg , let normal elections will be continue 
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = flg_Hindenburg
			}
				clr_country_flag = flg_Hindenburg
		}	
	# backout the occupy province as before
	#------GRE --------
	if = { 
		limit = {
			any_owned_province = {
				has_province_flag = flg_ger_back_GRE
			}
		}

				has_province_flag = flg_ger_back_GRE

clr_flag_temp = {
	if = {
		limit = { has_country_flag = flg_general_temp }
			clr_country_flag = flg_general_temp
	}	
	if = {
		limit = { has_country_flag = flg_wen_temp }
			clr_country_flag = flg_wen_temp
	}	
	if = {
		limit = { has_country_flag = flg_huan_temp }
			clr_country_flag = flg_huan_temp
	}	
	if = {
		limit = { has_country_flag = flg_relationship_temp	 }
			clr_country_flag = flg_relationship_temp	
	}	
}	

subtract_bit_mandate_effect = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_dlc = "Mandate of Heaven"
			is_emperor_of_china = yes
		}
		add_mandate = -1
	}
}

add_bit_mandate_effect = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_dlc = "Mandate of Heaven"
			is_emperor_of_china = yes
		}
		add_mandate = 1
	}
}

subtract_bit_meritocracy_effect = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_dlc = "Mandate of Heaven"
			is_emperor_of_china = yes
		}
		add_meritocracy = -1
	}
}

add_bit_meritocracy_effect = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_dlc = "Mandate of Heaven"
			is_emperor_of_china = yes
		}
		add_meritocracy = 1
	}
}

subtract_1_num_of_talking_wife = {
		if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				which = num_of_talking_wife
				value = 1
			}
		}
		subtract_variable = {
			which = num_of_talking_wife
			value = 1
		}	
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = {
				check_variable = {
					which = num_of_talking_wife
					value = 1
				}
			}
		}
		set_variable = {
			which = num_of_talking_wife
			value = 0
		}	
	}
}	

subtract_2_num_of_talking_wife = {
		if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				which = num_of_talking_wife
				value = 2
			}
		}
		subtract_variable = {
			which = num_of_talking_wife
			value = 2
		}	
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = {
				check_variable = {
					which = num_of_talking_wife
					value = 2
				}
			}
		}
		set_variable = {
			which = num_of_talking_wife
			value = 0
		}	
	}
}	

add_1_num_of_talking_wife = {
	change_variable = {
		which = num_of_talking_wife
		value = 1
	}
}	

add_2_num_of_talking_wife = {
	change_variable = {
		which = num_of_talking_wife
		value = 2
	}
}
